	* b3/config.py, b3/docs/LICENSE.txt, b3/lib/__init__.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/ElementInclude.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/ElementIron.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/ElementPath.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/ElementTree.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/HTMLTreeBuilder.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/SgmlopXMLTreeBuilder.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/SimpleXMLTreeBuilder.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/SimpleXMLWriter.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/TidyHTMLTreeBuilder.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/TidyTools.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/XMLTreeBuilder.py,
	b3/lib/elementtree/__init__.py: ElementTree is now in the 'lib'
	folder of the b3 directory. This is because many webhosts (the ideal
	host for remote B3) do not include ElementTree, and do not allow
	libraries to be installed. License information changed accordingly.
	ElementTree no longer required.

	tested.

2009-08-28  James 'Bakes' Baker <bakes@ymail.com>

	* b3/functions.py, b3/parser.py, b3/plugins/ftpytail.py: Added
	remote B3 ability.  In b3.xml, simply set the game_log path in the syntax:
	ftp://user:pass@host/path:logfilename, b3 will automatically
	download the file to your hard disk.  Basic functionality, if connection is lost, it should automatically
	restart, but it has not been tested, and if it was down for ten or
	more minutes on a populated server, there would certainly be severe
	problems. Expect a restart implementation within around 48 hours.  Signed-off-by: James 'Bakes' Baker <bakes@ymail.com>
